				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'SG', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20234441' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

												<img class="movie_thumb" src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/256819365/movie.184x123.jpg?t=1611420489">

                                                                    <div class="slider_ctn">
                                        <div id="highlight_slider_left" class="slider_left"><span></span></div>
                                        <div class="slider" id="highlight_slider">
                                            <div class="slider_bg">
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="handle" style="position: absolute; left: 0px;">
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div id="highlight_slider_right" class="slider_right"><span></span></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 3720;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

This file will copy from the default file on first run of VR.\n[*] Allowed the option to configure multiple files from the config application\n[*] Fixed various inconsistencies in config app where by changing adapter or monitor would lose any previous setting changes\n[*] Fixed windows version reporting in config app\n[*] Updated displaying of PC Specs to show only relevant information in config app\n[*] Removed various unused settings from config file\n[\/list]\n[b]Physics[\/b]\n[list]\n[*] Ensured that results files \/ ai report battery state when it\u2019s the primary energy source\n[*] Various fixes for battery energy consumption\n[\/list]\n[b]Graphics[\/b]\n[list]\n[*] Updated Dashboard Elements Shader to use IBL Setup for better lighting\n[*] Added LowLumEmissive shader to replace old Dashboard usage on track assets (Start\/Pit Lights etc) and in Car LEDs. The game will auto reassign these.\n[*] Updated Cockpit Readout format to allow offsets, to render multiple readouts to the same background\n[*] Added Cockpit Readout Icon format, which can render texture to background, with configurable number of elements, and options to change colours or uvw islands based on value, with options for Fuel, Battery, RPM, TC, TCActive, ABS, ABSLocked\n[*] Added various extra cockpit readouts: FuelLastLap, FuelFinishAverage, BatteryLastLap, BatteryFinishAverage, CurrentLap, Delta, TCSlip, TCCut, BatteryRegenLevel, ElectricMotorMap\n[*] Updated Moddev Tweak Bar displays for new options\n[*] Updated method for sharing if a rain light is active over network, to ensure better consistency when it is used to show in the pit lane, battery regen or due to the weather.\n[*] Enable rain light when battery is harvesting on throttle. Use CockpitInfo.ini params to configure:\n[*] RegenLightRequireThrottle=1\/0 (requires higher throttle than brake)\n[*] RegenLightMinPowerWatts=15000 (requires 15kw regen to show the light)\n[\/list]\n[b]AI[\/b]\n[list]\n[*] Reworked AI throttle behaviour\n[*] Less overshooting, more controlled deceleration\n[*] Improved acceleration with less wheelspin\n[*] Improved corner exits\n[*] Eliminated even more sources of oscillation\n[*] Improved laptimes for certain vehicles\n[*] Pit speed limit won\u2019t be overshot\n[*] Stop positions (grid, pit box) will no longer be overshot\n[*] Reworked AI reaction to other vehicles (road courses)\n[*] AI will now properly slipstream other vehicles\n[*] Overtaking occurs if AI can achieve overlap before the next corner, otherwise the AI will save fuel\n[*] Multiclass: Faster classes will no longer slow down when trying to overtake slower classes\n[*] Multiclass: Faster classes avoid overtaking unless they can get fully past before the apex\n[*] Multiclass: Faster classes will attempt to carry more momentum, and lift off early if no overtaking opportunity exists\n[*] AI will now be more cautious when other cars are around\n[*] AI can now use more of the space following other cars, for proper drafting behaviour\n[*] More cautious when yellow flags are ahead or under FCY\n[*] Player and other cars will no longer be rear ended unless a sudden unexpected lane change makes a reaction impossible\n[*] When cars ahead are in a fight, AI will now set up for an overtake on corner exit\n[*] AI won\u2019t hesitate to go 3-wide if the situation allows for it, but will pull out before the next braking zone if an overtake seems too dangerous\n[*] Less incident prone with large grids\n[\/list]\n[b]HUD[\/b]\n[list]\n[*] Updated Default HUD with multiple options for different element combinations\n[*] Added Battery State & Usage options, as well as LEDs for P2P and 						<div id="game_area_description" class="game_area_description">
							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							<h2 class="bb_tag">Summary</h2><br>rFactor 2 is a realistic, easily extendable racing simulation from Studio 397. It offers the latest in vehicle and race customization, great graphics, outstanding multiplayer and the height of racing realism. rFactor 2 features mixed class road racing with ultra realistic dynamics, an immersive sound environment and stunning graphics, perfect for top-level esports and a rich single-player experience.<br><br>Race against a field of AI cars, or in multi-player mode against others. rFactor 2 supports a full day-night cycle as well as dynamically varying weather conditions such as rain which dynamically builds into puddles. Tracks feature "real-road" technology that changes the grip as more cars drive on it. You can run full 24 hour endurance events and in multi-player mode, driver swaps are also supported. Everything can be customized by the community, including adding new tracks and cars, and a wealth of add-ons are available on-line.Working with several partners, rFactor 2 has been used in hundreds of esport championships all over the world – in particular McLaren’s World’s Fastest Gamer and Formula E.<br><br>rFactor 2 is also an evolving product, which will be updated and added to for many years, so the list of features will expand!<h2 class="bb_tag">Features</h2><br><strong>Physics</strong><br><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>Updated to use multi-core CPU technology<br></li><li>Advanced physics engine<br></li><li>Newly updated tyre model<br></li><li>Driving surface construction, even painted line thickness, affects grip levels<br></li><li>Engine boost and Turbo modeling<br></li><li>Complex aerodynamics<br></li><li>Head physics, cockpit vibrations, detailed bump modeling</li></ul><br><strong>Dynamic Racing Experience</strong><br><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>Real-time day/night lighting transitions<br></li><li>Realistic wet/dry weather transitions<br></li><li>Dynamically laid rubber increases grip throughout racing session(s)<br></li><li>Rubber chunks (“marbles”) roll off tyres and can affect grip<br></li><li>Tyres sustain damage from poor driving (such as "flatspotting" a tyre) or setups, affecting grip immediately and over time<br></li><li>Dynamically drying racing line after rain<br></li><li>Environments filled with animated events like planes, flag marshalls and more…</li></ul><br><strong>Graphics/Sound</strong><br><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>Real-time day/night lighting transitions<br></li><li>Projected headlights for night time driving<br></li><li>Open VR support for multiple headsets<br></li><li>Look to apex and head motion tracking support<br></li><li>DX11 advanced graphics engine<br></li><li>Real-time day/night transitions<br></li><li>Adjust player and opponent volume ratio<br></li><li>See the apex with the Look Ahead slider<br></li><li>Adjust your seat and mirror while in the driver’s seat<br></li><li>Updating real-time scoring towers<br></li><li>Expanded and enhanced gauge and LCD features for vehicle cockpits<br></li><li>Improved loading times<br></li><li>Updated sound engine<br></li><li>Changing engine sounds based on upgraded vehicle performance</li></ul><br><strong>Gameplay</strong><br><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>New AI who will race for and defend positions<br></li><li>Define AI opponent types, strength and aggression<br></li><li>Races can be lap based, time based or both<br></li><li>Vehicle upgrade system that affects both the appearance and performance of a vehicle</li></ul><br><strong>Camera/Replays</strong><br><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>“Resume from Replay” allows you to resume a race from a saved replay<br></li><li>Full screen monitor and ability to rewind<br></li><li>Freely move camera from any position including the ever famous exclusive Swingman<br></li><li>Spectator mode</li></ul><br><strong>Multiplayer</strong><br><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>Opponent car skins automatically transmitted<br></li><li>Completely new multiplayer engine<br></li><li>Dedicated server<br></li><li>Native voting system<br></li><li>Add AI to multiplayer games<br></li><li>Boot and ban player lists that can be passed around<br></li><li>Security checks to combat potential cheating</li></ul><br><strong>Open Architecture</strong><br><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>Support for modder created car,track and plugin content<br></li><li>Fully adjustable Showroom, UI and HUD layouts<br></li><li>More Plugin Interfaces<br></li><li>Easy to use customizable multi-language support<br></li><li>Rules to simulate different types of racing<br></li><li>Completely customize your 	<div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" class="review_box    partial">
		<div id="ReviewContentsummary19475002">
			
			<div class="leftcol" id="ReviewContentsummary19475002_leftcol">
				<div class="avatar">
					<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/sephiat/">

					</a>
				</div>
				<div class="persona_name"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/sephiat/" data-miniprofile="111166782">Sephi-AtStudio</a></div>
								<div class="num_owned_games"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/sephiat/games/?tab=all">帐户内拥有 242 项产品</a></div>
												<div class="num_reviews"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/sephiat/recommended/">5 篇评测</a></div>

			<div class="rightcol" id="ReviewContentsummary19475002_rightcol">
								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/sephiat/recommended/365960/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">
					<div class="thumb">
						<img id="votingImage" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_thumbsUp_v6.png" width="40" height="40">
													<img class="responsive_voting_image" src="https://community.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/images/apphubs/bigpicture/thumbs_upselected.png" width="40" height="40">
											</div>

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 2,860.5 小时												（评测时 303.3 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary19475002_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2015 年 12 月 4 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					f1c和rF1几乎伴我度过了整个高中和大学，从OFCR、SFCR到OFRL、FFL、EAF1、CNSTEA、CSTCC再到CNR，几乎国内大大小小的联赛都曾短暂停留，国内的SIM Racing开始走下坡路后，也尝试开始转向幕后专攻赛道MOD开发，无论是失败的澳大利亚阿尔伯特公园赛道、曾一时惊艳国内的新加坡滨海湾赛道、10天国内闪电首发的俄罗斯索契赛道，也不论是无限期跳票的菲奥拉诺、穆杰罗、纽伯格林、阿尔加维甚至到现在进度停滞的rF2版新加坡滨海湾，每一条赛道都倾注了完全的热情，真是一段快乐的时光。<br><br>两年前rF2刚出第一个Beta版的时候就已经开始关注、测试和尝试MOD开发了，不过由于当时的技术限制和rF2本身的优化影响，到了去年才真正开始着手。这次rF2登录Steam，作为ISI的信仰级SIM Racing作品，也是第一时间就入手了本体和终身在线使用权，虽然感觉Steam Edition版的rF2没有D版的运行起来方便，不过各种官方MOD的下载和创意工坊的订阅都颇为方便，可谓有利有弊吧。自主MOD安装目前还没有尝试过，不过看文件结构应该是支持的，相信日后的开发过程会更为顺利。<br><br>建议直接购买rFactor 2 with Lifetime Subscription，两个本体的价格，但是终身联机使用权这项特权省去了每年额外的联机使用权费用，真的很划算。<br><br>================华丽的日期分割线================<br><br>2018年<br>rF2已经完全由397接收了，更新了DX11（尽管效果还比较一般），取消了需要另外购买的联机授权，现在只要拥有本体就能够联机了。<br><br>过去两三个月都在尝试转模开发墨尔本的街道赛，不过后来因为学画画搁浅了，目前处于停工状态，不过早起beta版已上架创意工坊（仅好友可访问），现阶段对我这种玩家而言已经十分满足，日常的开放程度依旧是最大特点，剩下的大概就是这条墨尔本什么时候能完工了[/笑]<br><br>================华丽的日期分割线================<br><br>2019年底2020年初又开始重新开坑决定把那条始终做不完的墨尔本阿尔伯特公园赛道坐进来，大概前期中期已经完成80%，在油管和B站也上传了几个测试视频，但是这时候才发现了一个不是很严重但是强迫症的我无法忍受的问题（有关二级贴图，虽然设置好渲染已经能让模型在游戏里有一个还不错的画面表现，但是加上二级贴图以后会给模型本身带来一个不错的效果提升），所以3月中旬决定重做大部分的渲染，很不巧此时开始准备复工而且与Inspeed Racing应斯赛车的合作导致手头工作比较多没有时间再顾得上这条赛道，很遗憾，这条跳票数次的墨尔本阿尔伯特公园赛道又要暂时搁置了。<br><br>（讲道理我应该是第一个在rF1 / rF2里实现练习赛排位赛 / 正赛发车灯有不同表现的MOD制作人了）<br><br>希望不久以后能把这条赛道完结吧。<br><br>================华丽的日期分割线================<br><br>2021年2月17日<br>这两个月重新开始填墨尔本阿尔伯特公园赛道的坑，大部分关键模型的PBR化已经完成，剩下一些边边角角的模型（比如马修的亭子，路边卡车之类的），路面的PBR并不完整，之后还要研究研究RDT的UV，实在不行就这样发也是可能的，很多进度的截图和视频都在B站有更新，ID：抖SA酱<br><br>================华丽的日期分割线================<br><br>2021年8月8日<br>重新做了整个路面的Detail，现在刹车印的UV层是最合理的状态了，这条墨尔本剩下的工作并不多了，相信很快就能做完并且发布了<br><br>================华丽的日期分割线================<br><br>2022年4月7日<br>澳大利亚阿尔伯特公园赛道2019布局（包含F1的大奖赛和supercars的墨尔本400两种布局）正式上架steam创意工坊，面向所有rFactor 2玩家免费开放<br>（看了一下上条进度更新居然是去年7月了，其实肝一点去年9月完全可以做好发布，但是去年8月开始入坑原神了，垃圾氪金手游，骗我钱财！）<br><br>================华丽的日期分割线================<br><br>2022年4月22日<br>Albert Park 2019订阅数超过2500，感谢各位的支持					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary90447012_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2021 年 4 月 17 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					这游戏也就硬核中的硬核才能接受了吧，优点很优秀，缺点很致命<br>轮胎物理在几个能玩到的模拟器里算是最强<br>手感舒服，很清晰很干脆，个人觉得很接近真实，算是几个赛车模拟游戏中最好的了<br>当车轮抱死，能明显感受到车胎在地上的滑动与摩擦，得益于此，当车失控我能感受到车身的变化，从而快速地做出补救<br>最明显的是前驱车的驾驶，当深踩油门时，前轮拽着车身前进的感受直接反馈到手里的方向盘上，太舒服了，玩的很快乐。我乐此不疲地这样玩了一下午，地板油乱甩方向<br>缺点也很明显，一是画质，不知道是哪一部分做的不好，就是很奇怪。有时画面看着很真实，有时又很假，而且调色让人眼睛很快变得疲惫，这一点可太要命了<br>游戏界面估计直接是工程师做的吧，无论老版还是新版本，槽点一堆，都不想吐槽了<br>二来dlc是比较贵的，而且mod不多，厂商有意向iracing的模式靠拢。当然，贵是我的缺点。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

					发布于：2020 年 2 月 8 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					【内核、优势】<br>rf2引擎本身硬核 是需要高端盘子玩的 拟真赛车沙盒<br>rf2是最接近金字塔顶尖绝对老大iRacing 且不需点卡式联网的了<br>即便同类中 口碑优秀到爆炸的ac 与rf2也有小小差距<br><br>【劣势】<br>rf2的赛道和车辆数量 是一大弱点<br>主要靠创意工坊 质量好的就那么几个 挑选也比较心累<br>操作上 UI 车队 进站等 用盘子可能不太方便 设置也比较繁琐<br><br>【对比】<br>比起ac少了大厂味 游戏味<br>ac画质甚至可以当做吹点<br>ac动不动就法拉利全家 带F1 纽北实地全扫描赛道 各种授权<br>ac用盘子可以解决全部操作 不用离手 包括驾驶 UI 车队和进站操作 定义key简单<br>而forza系列，gt系列，dirt系列，Project CARS系列，Drive Club，F1游戏系列等并非死磕物理到极致真实，追求模拟级别的游戏，它们更偏向赛车文化性，游戏性，故应该当做“邻种”，强行对比只能互相伤害<br><br>【个人感悟】<br>毕竟早就过了年少爱研究的年纪<br>本来是为了体验游戏乐趣 结果去收集一堆 mod数据和风评 设置各种奇怪参数<br>完全脱离了黑盒娱乐宗旨 成了灰盒甚至白盒 游戏不知不觉变成了“商研”<br>现在看来 这只是一种变向的控制欲罢了 企图撬开黑盒 操了不该操的心<br><br>【个人理解、意见】<br>作为有赛车梦想的圈外人士<br>rf2精神地位比较高 如果不怕折腾和反人类 可以入手<br>但是 更加强推 物理引擎毫不示弱 且其他方面吊打rf2的ac(Assetto Corsa)<br>ac是纯粹的快乐，rf2是近乎偏执的抑扬式体验<br><br>【升华】<br>最后，不必遵循我，也不建议遵循任何家伙<br>祝你在模拟赛车海洋里 找到自己内心想要的<br>游戏愉快！					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="content">
					1，这是个非常棒非常拟真的模拟类赛车游戏，要买的话建议搞个方向盘先。<br><br>2，物理比ac好，画质比ac差。（ac指 assetto corsa ，不知道ac的话可以理解为这游戏物理超真实，画质辣鸡。。。）<br><br>3，车子大多是是赛车好多都不认识（甚至货车和全地形车都有。。。），ac里面都是量产车就亲切多了。<br><br>4，自带mod管理器，可以下载些车和地图玩，比如去网上找个北环装上跑跑。<br><br>5，支持创意工坊。<br><br>6，建议买rFactor 2 with Lifetime Subscription这个版本，终身线上服务。<br><br>  -------------------------------------------------------------------------<br><br>ps：可能这游戏里的车都用序列手动变速箱吧，踩不踩离合都能挂上档（转速不匹配的时候也可以），郁闷。。。					<div class="gradient"></div>
